Grand Confucius Ceremony in Qufu; Most of the Ancient Music in the Confucius Temple Is Incomplete; Chairman Lin's Eulogy Has Been Delivered

Jinan Correspondence: Qufu is the birthplace of the former teacher Confucius and the place where his sacred body rests. The legacy and artifacts are all there, and they are all related to the culture and history of the East. For this year's Confucius birthday commemoration ceremony, the Chairman of the National Government, Lin Sen, specially wrote an eulogy and sent Han Fuqu, Chairman of the Shandong Provincial Government, as his representative to offer sacrifices. For the sake of careful worship and reverence for his predecessor, Han pre-appointed Li Shuchun, Director of the Department of Civil Affairs, and He Siyuan, Director of the Department of Education, to go to Qufu on a special train on the 25th to prepare everything. The reporter also went to observe the ceremony. Han himself also came south by special train on the 25th and will arrive before 7:00 AM on the 27th. On the afternoon of the 26th, He Siyuan and the artists who came to observe the ceremony, such as Liu Haisu, visited the Confucius Forest, paid respects at the Confucius Temple, Yan Temple, and Shao Hao Mausoleum, and other sacred sites. At about 5:00 PM, Li Shuchun, He Siyuan, and other participants in the ceremony rehearsed the rituals at the Confucius Temple. Confucius's sacrificial official, Kong Decheng, will go to Yanzhou on the 27th to welcome Han. The grand Confucius sacrifice ceremony will be solemnly held at the Confucius Temple in Qufu at 7:00 AM on the 27th.

The reporter learned the text of Chairman Lin's eulogy to Confucius from the ceremonial preparatory office. The text reads: "On the 27th day of the eighth month of the 25th year of the Republic of China, Lin Sen, Chairman of the National Government, specially sent Han Fuqu, Chairman of the Shandong Provincial Government, to offer sacrifices to the spirit of the former teacher Confucius. Only the former teacher's Tao surpassed the past and present, and his virtues illuminated both China and foreign countries. With the sacredness of innate versatility, he established rules that had never existed for the people, selected the virtuous and capable, and made the world a public place. The Great Harmony was initiated, integrating the mind and governing in peace, consistently adhering to the principles of rectitude. With reverence, on the occasion of the anniversary of his birth, we perform the ceremony of sacrifice. Like a pearl balance and red thread, we remember the image at Mount Ni. Like jade chime and golden sound, we follow the rites and music at the Si River. May you enjoy the sacrifice."

The Confucius Temple used to use ancient musical instruments for the Confucius sacrifice, but now they are incomplete. The reporter visited Kong Lingshu, the director of the Ancient Music Training Institute, to inquire about how many types of ancient musical instruments there are, how many of each type, and whether the playing methods are still transmitted. According to Kong (Lingshu), there are six qin and four se, all of which have been lost. All six dongxiao and dizi sheng are complete. Two guan, four chi, chi have been lost. Zhu yu and kuo fu·tao drum are each two are complete. Tian drum two, Ying drum one, foot drum one, are complete, Suspended drum one has been lost. Bo bell one, bianzhong sixteen, teqing one, are complete. Bianqing sixteen, have been half-lost. He also said that Hunan still has a complete set of ancient musical instruments. When the institute's finances are sufficient, they will go to Hunan to visit and try to complete them. Otherwise, in a few years, the playing methods of ancient music will be lost, and there will be the regret of not being able to play them.

Subsequently, he visited Confucius's sacrificial official, Kong Decheng, and asked about his recent life and the date of his marriage to Ms. Sun Qifang, as reported in the news. According to Kong, his daily life is mostly uneventful, except for reading. Recently, due to the hot weather, he only reads for six hours a day. In addition to the Spring and Autumn Annals and the classics, he also studies arithmetic, history, and geography. Regarding his research on reading the classics, he felt that Liu Xin was a thief of the classics. Liu Xin was a member of the Han imperial family and the son of Liu Xiang. He led the collection of secret texts and divided the six arts and books into seven abstracts, creating the beginning of later generations' catalogs of classics and books. He planned to list the Zuo Zhuan and the Mao Poetry as official studies, which was criticized by later scholars. Kong criticized Liu for this. He also talked about Han Chairman (Fuqu) advocating the Confucian Association, which showed respect and admiration. Not only is the Kong clan grateful, but also the people of the whole country. At a time when the Confucian path is declining, it is necessary to advocate and urgently seek restoration. The dispute over the sacrifice fields in Sishui was also completely resolved by Chairman Han sending Zhang Senyi (Shouqian). As for his marriage to Sun Qifang, it is purely in accordance with old etiquette and entirely based on matchmakers. The previous report that Zhang Zongchang's daughter proposed to him when he was Governor of Shandong in the 17th year of the Republic of China is not true. At that time, he was only seven years old and could not talk about marriage. It is now scheduled to be held in November of the lunar calendar, but the location, whether in Jinan or Qufu, has not yet been determined.

Recent Situation in Chahar North and Suiyuan East

Beiping Dispatch, Talk from a Guest from Suiyuan: Since the bandit troops in Chahar North were repelled after invading Suiyuan East, foreign sources have paid close attention to the situation in Suiyuan and believe that the situation in Suiyuan is extremely tense. In fact, the people in the provincial capital of Suiyuan, as well as Jining, Fengzhen, and other counties, are very stable, and the business situation is as before, not as serious as rumored. However, the hidden crisis in Suiyuan Province is an undeniable fact. The five counties in Suiyuan East (Jining, Taolin, Xinghe, Fengzhen, and Liangcheng) are close to Chahar North. Jining is only ninety li away from Shangdu, and Xinghe is very close to Zhangbei, only thirty li away. It can be reached by car in half an hour. Currently, the outposts of Suiyuan East and Chahar North are only a dozen li apart. There are a total of ten thousand troops stationed in Suiyuan. In Suiyuan East, there is a part of Li Fuying's two divisions, Zhao Chengshou's cavalry, Fu Zuoyi's infantry, and Zhou Dai's artillery. The officials and people of Suiyuan Province unanimously expressed that they will never give way to anyone who disturbs the security of the province and vow to fight to the end. Baotou is also peaceful, but Japanese planes often travel back and forth between Ping and Bao, and two or three Japanese planes are stationed in Baotou for a long time.

In Chahar North, after the six counties of Zhangbei, Guyuan, Shangdu, Baochang, Kangbao, and Huade were occupied by puppet troops, bandits gathered in large numbers, including Li Shouxin, Zhuoshikai, Wang Ying, Su Meilong, and others. After they arrived, they changed Jiabu Temple to Dehua (i.e., changed the province to Huade) County, and Daqinggou to Shangyi County. As for the puppet army's defense area, Li Shouxin is stationed in Shangdu with more than three thousand troops, and only two-thirds of them have guns. Their organization is three companies per regiment, and each company has only fifty people. Su Meilong's bandits originally had more than a thousand troops, but now they have been incorporated by Wang Ying. Wang Daoyi's bandit troops claim to have two to three thousand people. After the failure of the recent invasion of Suiyuan East, they suffered heavy losses and are now retreating to the four rural areas and the Baitazi area for reorganization. Wang Ying's troops only have a little over a thousand people, with both Mongolian and puppet troops, which is quite chaotic. Currently, the puppet army is actively extorting horses and forcibly conscripting laborers in Chahar North. It is expected that the bandit army will invade Suiyuan East again. The Chief of Staff of the Japanese Kwantung Army, Seishiro Itagaki, flew to Suiyuan on the 25th, and his mission is likely to inquire about everything so that he can prepare for corresponding steps. In Kangbao, there is also a Mongolian military training center set up by De Wang, with two to three thousand new recruits, who were also forcibly conscripted and are currently being trained.

According to another dispatch from Zhangjiakou, De Wang, under pressure from a certain party, contacted Li Shouxin, Wang Ying, Zhang HaiPeng and others, in order to launch a large-scale attack on Suiyuan, and scheduled a military conference at Bailingmiao on September 2nd to discuss the steps for invading Suiyuan East. At that time, De Wang, Li Shouxin, Wang Ying, and Zhang Haipeng will all participate. Currently, within fifteen li around Jiabu Temple, the puppet army is raping, plundering, and looting, which is unspeakable, but they are better to merchants. Currently, merchants from Zhangyuan have opened stores in Jiabu Temple, and sales have been quite extensive recently. A lot of goods have been transported from Zhangyuan in recent days. A certain party issued military pay to the bandits on the 25th, and it was decided that the bandit troops would move westward on the 26th. The troops receiving pay in Jiabu Temple included the subordinates of the Mongolian soldiers Li Shouxin, Wang Ying, Zhang Haipeng, etc. (26th)

Zhangyuan Cao Lun Greedily Rented Out House to Foreigners, Arrested and Sent to Bureau, Fined 600 Yuan

Zhangjiakou Communication: In recent months, during the eventful autumn in Chahar North, certain foreigners in Zhangyuan have been arrogant and domineering, doing whatever they want, and it has been quite difficult to maintain local security. Recently, a resident named Cao Lun had an empty house in Fengjia Garden and privately rented the house to the Qiaodong Zhongyuan Chamber of Commerce (operated by certain foreigners) for a rent of 400 yuan, without reporting it to the Public Security Bureau beforehand. On the night of the 20th, the Zhongyuan Chamber of Commerce sent people to clean the house, and they were discovered by the duty police of the Third District Public Security Bureau. They immediately reported to the sub-bureau, and the sub-bureau chief sent policemen to take Cao Lun and a group of offenders to the bureau and transferred them to the Provincial Public Security Bureau for interrogation. After repeated interrogations by the Provincial Public Security Bureau, Cao Lun admitted that he privately rented the house to foreigners without concealment. The Public Security Bureau planned to fine him 600 yuan to repair the city's standard clock, and it has now been submitted to the Provincial Government for approval. (25th)

The Widely Circulated Revenge Case of the Wronged Ghost in Chao-Shan

Shantou Communication: Huang Ashuang of Dazhubao, Fourth District, Meixian County, was a moderately wealthy man who had a long-standing feud with his cousin Huang Taode over a family property dispute. On February 29th of the 21st year of the Republic of China, Taode colluded with bandits, broke into the house and killed Huang Ashuang. Huang Ashuang's wife, Zhong, was also stabbed in multiple places, and all the property was looted. Huang Taode then fled with the bandits. After a long time, he returned home and falsely claimed that he had also been kidnapped by bandits. It was found that his family was poor and had no money to redeem him, so he was released. Huang Zhong knew that he colluded with bandits to commit the crime and kill her husband, but she dared not say it openly. Later, the district office discovered that Taode was highly suspected and detained him in the county government. The former county magistrate, Peng Jingyi, sentenced him to ten years in prison and reported it to the headquarters of the First Army Group for handling. The headquarters believed that there were many suspicious points in the case's confession, so it rejected it for retrial in order to determine the crime. Subsequently, due to changes in the Guangdong situation, the case was repeatedly delayed. On the 18th of this month, County Magistrate Liang Hanzhao summoned a group of witnesses and held a trial at night. Chief Judge Han sat in court and summoned Zhong for questioning. Zhong suddenly changed her state, and her actions and accent were just like Huang Ashuang appearing in person. She spoke in a man's voice and confessed how Huang Taode colluded with the bandits to commit the crime, where he hid afterward, and every detail was as vivid as a picture. Chief Judge Han and the people who were recording the confession in court were all moved and changed color. Zhong also described Taode's words and actions in the bandits' place, the names of the bandits, and how the stolen silver was distributed, all one by one. However, Taode still sophistically argued that Zhong was suffering from a mental illness and that what she said could not be completely believed. Before he finished speaking, Taode's face suddenly changed greatly, and he spat out white phlegm. He also spoke in Ashuang's accent and cursed Huang Taode for being so devoid of conscience and how he committed the crime and how he fled, revealing all kinds of circumstances. Chief Judge Han was so frightened that his face turned pale, and beads of sweat rolled down his forehead. The person recording the confession trembled and could not record. Chief Judge Han hurriedly left the court and went inside, intending to ask County Magistrate Liang for instructions on how to sentence the crime in order to comfort the wronged soul. At that time, County Magistrate Liang had been eavesdropping behind the screen after receiving a report from the people standing in court. Han entered, and Liang ordered him to quickly leave the court to avoid such strange things from happening again, which could not be dealt with. So, he shackled Taode and imprisoned him in the county government. The people in the county government were frightened all night, and no one dared to close their eyes. The next day, County Magistrate Liang summoned Huang Zhong to the inner court. Because her situation was pitiful, he specially issued 50 yuan in condolence money to send her home and sentenced Huang Taode to the most severe punishment. He reported to Yu Hanmou, the commander-in-chief of the Fourth Route Army, for approval by telegram. On the 24th, Taode's identity was verified, and he was escorted to the execution ground and shot to death in public to warn the masses. This revenge case of the wronged ghost spread throughout Chao-Mei. (24th)

Taiwanese Smugglers Beat and Insult Xiamen Customs Officers, Two Seriously Injured and More Than Ten Slightly Injured

Xiamen Communication: The Japanese ship Fujian Maru arrived in Xiamen from Taiwan on the morning of the 26th. More than ten customs officers, including the British Deputy Inspector of the Outer Section, Yi Wannafu, and inspectors Pan Dehua, Wu Chuntai, Xu Daozu, Huang Yipei, Chen Shaoyi, Sun Dajing, and Han Shikui, went down to the ship for inspection. In the clothes and pants pockets of a certain smuggler from Taiwan, they found more than twenty fountain pens and immediately detained them, ordering him to pay taxes. The smuggler refused to pay taxes and tried to snatch them back. The customs officers refused, so he started beating them. At that time, there were many Taiwanese smugglers on the ship, who rushed forward and surrounded the customs officers. They used baseball bats, cymbals, and other weapons to beat them. One of the customs officers broke free and went to see the captain, asking him to send a radio message to the customs radio station and to signal with flags and blow the whistle more than twenty times to notify the customs to come to the rescue. At this time, the ship was moored at sea. Upon receiving the news, the Customs Commissioner immediately telegraphed the Japanese Consul to jointly board the ship with three members of the Japanese consulate and two British customs officers on a speedboat. Only then did they disperse the Taiwanese smugglers who were beating people, arrest five Taiwanese perpetrators, and take them back to the Japanese consulate. The customs confiscated twenty fountain pens, and the weapons used in the attack were also brought back as evidence for negotiations. The Customs Commissioner believed that the Taiwanese smugglers had repeatedly beaten and insulted customs officers, which was illegal, and immediately lodged a protest with the Japanese Consul, demanding: (1) Punishment of the perpetrators; (2) Guarantee that similar incidents will not happen in the future. Negotiations are currently underway. Chen Shaoyi and Huang Yipei were the most seriously injured among the injured customs officers, and the rest were slightly injured. According to doctors, Chen and Huang need long-term treatment to recover. As for the so-called "smugglers," they are people who carry goods on ships and specialize in smuggling. (August 27th)

Songjiang: Pu Mengjiu Arrives in Songjiang for a Mission

Pu Mengjiu from the Investigation Department of the Central Party Headquarters arrived in Songjiang yesterday on official business. According to Pu, the Central Government is paying close attention to the participation of party members in rural labor service this time. The current central work of the department focuses on the investigation of rural society and the distribution of party members in rural centers in order to mobilize party members to promote rural economic construction movements.

Taicang: Cotton Selection Demonstration

Mixed cotton selection is the easiest and most effective method for farmers to keep good seeds and maintain cotton quality. The Agricultural Group of the Tai-Jia-Bao Agricultural Improvement Research Association, in view of the lack of this habit among farmers in the three counties, initiated a mixed cotton selection movement and specially held a public demonstration in the cotton field of the association's experimental field every afternoon. As for the theory and detailed methods of seed selection, a special agricultural publication has been compiled for consultation. Those in other areas who wish to request guidance from the association are also willing to provide services.

Wuxi: Giant Black Fish Discovered

Behind Zhou Pai Lane, Seventh Bao, Yangdong Township, Third District, outside the South Gate, there is an unattended pond with an area of about three mu. The northern part is two zhang deep and as clear as a mirror. Recently, a giant fish was suddenly discovered in the pond, with a jet-black body, a head as big as a dipper, and a length of seven or eight chi, floating in the center of the pond, raising its head and spraying water towards the sun. When it was glimpsed by the villagers, it was immediately spread throughout the village, and those who saw it marveled at it. However, when the giant fish heard human voices, it would dive to the bottom of the water and not come out for a long time. Currently, the residents of the village are planning to drain the pond and find a way to catch it.

Ningbo: Cargo Boat Robbed by Bandits

Pu Gezui in Xihu Port, Xiangshan, is a mooring place for merchant ships. Cargo boats from various places gather to load and transport passengers and goods. The other day, two boats from Qiangtou and Huangxi set sail one after another after picking up passengers from the port. Unexpectedly, when they sailed to the waters of Dachanzui near Xiasha, they suddenly saw four bandit ships coming head-on. The cargo boats tried to escape but were unable to do so and were robbed. The two boats were robbed of more than 3,000 yuan of passengers' goods and cash. After the bandits were full, they set sail and left. The two boats sailed back to Qiangtou and Huangxi. Because the passengers were terrified, they were in a panic when they landed.

Pinghu: Slaughtering of Ploughing Cattle in Xindai

This year, the whole county had a bumper harvest. In Xindai Town, a group of ruffians incited the slaughter of cattle to sell meat. Initially, hot pot restaurants were set up in the southern township, and recently, they have extended to the northern township. The money from selling cattle is used for gambling. Since the Republic of China, the town has strictly prohibited the private slaughter of ploughing cattle, and there have been results for twenty years. Unfortunately, the trend of killing cattle has resurged this year. It is said that the Xindai Town District Office has ordered police officers to investigate and arrest them.

Shangyu: District Committee Summoned Opium Offenders

In the afternoon of the 25th of this month, two members of the Shaoxing District Security Command suddenly came to the county government with secret orders, stating that Wang Wulie, the fifth section chief of the county government, and Huang Langyuan, the former director of the Shangyu Opium Suppression Institute of the Shaoxing District Security Command, were suspected of smoking opium. The Executive Yuan secretly ordered the Zhejiang Provincial Security Command to instruct the District Command to come to Yu to summon them. It is said that County Magistrate Chen Daxun accompanied the district committee and a group of offenders to Hangzhou that day.

Attempted Murder of Husband

Shi Zhenhua, a resident of Yindong, is 33 years old and works as a farmer. He married a Wang woman from the same village as his wife. She is 26 years old this year. Wang is naturally shrewish and often treats her husband like a slave. The other night, after the couple had a verbal dispute over a trivial matter, Wang took advantage of her husband's sleep and stabbed him in the throat with sharp scissors. Zhenhua screamed in pain and was rescued by neighbors who heard the sound. Wang, fearing punishment, went downstairs and tried to commit suicide with the scissors, but was also rescued by neighbors. Zhenhua specially dragged Wang to the nearby police station to report her and transferred her to the court for trial.

Cixi: Loan Settlement for the Purchase of American Species

The Cixi-Huai County Cotton Transportation and Marketing Cooperative Union borrowed 10,000 yuan from the Kenye Bank for the purchase of American cotton. The contract was signed yesterday with County Magistrate Dai as the guarantor. The bank will pay 20,000 yuan in advance. When the cooperative receives cotton from the tenant farmers, the bank will pay the estimated value. The cooperative will repay the full amount after the last batch of American cotton is sold. The deadline is set for five months.

Wenzhou: Severe Drought and Rampant Epidemic

In the counties of Pingyang, Yuhuan, Leqing, etc. under Wenzhou, the weather has been extremely hot and there has been no rain for the past month. The late rice cannot be irrigated due to the depletion of river water. The soil is cracked and the rice stalks are like burning. This year's autumn harvest will be hopeless. The farmers are heartbroken and anxious. They have set up altars to pray for rain. In Yu Township, Pingyang, due to the drought, there is a panic over drinking water. Recently, cholera has suddenly been discovered, and the number of deaths has reached seven or eight.

Letter: Letter from Shen Youyi of Jiading

"Recently, I read the Jiading local news column in your newspaper on August 25, which mentioned that the central school was destroyed. After investigation, it does not conform to the facts at the time. According to Youyi, the brothers Youkang and Jin Guobao have always been friends. In the afternoon of the 23rd, at the Malu Central School, they talked to Jin Guobao about the fact that they had previously asked Jin to dredge the county education bureau, and the bureau did not hire him for not attending the lecture. Jin became ashamed and angry because Youkang mentioned the misspelled word in Jin's letter to the former teaching director, which led to a quarrel. As for the destruction and leading the rogues, the teachers of the school were all indoors at the time, which can prove that this did not happen. What your newspaper reported, I think it is a mistake of hearsay. I specially write to ask for correction. Shen Youyi" Qi, August 26, Correspondence address, Jiading Private Chengde School.

Estimate of German Combat Power (Part 2)

— by French General ×, translated by Yue Qi

Finally, let us examine the raw materials for manufacturing military supplies—such as metals, yarns, rubber, fuel, and oil—and the factories that use these raw materials to make guns, cannons, cloths, tires, gasoline, and ammunition. In other words, let us examine Germany's industrial capabilities.

Germany's iron metal production was originally not developed. The loss of the Lorraine mines has reduced its metal resources by two-thirds compared to before the Great War. Currently, out of the annual iron ore consumption of 16,700,000 tons, 6,000,000 tons are produced domestically, and the rest are imported from abroad. After the successful mining of iron ore in Palatinate and South Baden, the annual output can be increased by one million tons. But in any case, domestic production is never enough to meet consumption.

Of course, Germany is importing a large amount of steel to prevent the risk of being sealed off during wartime, but half of it is supplied by France, which is its enemy in future wars, and it is questionable whether this large supply will last. The supply from other countries—mainly Sweden—accounts for only a small number and cannot make up for its lack during wartime.

Germany has almost no copper mines; the copper mines of the Manslield Company only supply 10% of consumption: in 1934, out of the total consumption of 287,000 tons, only 28,000 tons were produced domestically. Imports supplied by the United States, South Africa, Belgian Congo, Chile, and other countries will stop when the war starts; no matter how sufficient the reserves are, there is no doubt that they will soon run out. Germany is well aware of this danger, so it is working hard to replace copper with aluminum and other metals it lacks—such as zinc and tin.

Germany is the world's largest aluminum producer. In 1933, the output reached 18,000 tons; in 1934, it reached 46,000 tons; in 1935, it reached 52,000 tons. But it lacks the raw materials for making aluminum. Its bauxite and cryolite production is almost zero: in 1929, bauxite production was only 7,300 tons; in 1934, bauxite imports reached 326,500 tons. To prevent its main suppliers (France, Hungary, Yugoslavia, Italy) from stopping supplies during wartime, Germany is working hard to extract aluminum from the mud in its own soil. According to German newspapers, this problem has been solved, but the facts proving this news have not yet appeared.

Germany's textile raw materials are very scarce. At most, only 10% of the total consumption of flax and hemp is supplied by the country; natural silk and cotton are almost non-existent. Therefore, Germany has to find ways to remedy this, such as expanding the area of flax cultivation, increasing wool production, manufacturing rayon, and inventing mixed grain textile fabrics.

As for coal, we can observe it from two figures: the annual consumption is 275,000,000 tons; the annual output is 181,000,000 tons.

Germany's Thuringia and Hanover are famous throughout the country for their oil production, and there are many oil wells there. In recent years, their output has quadrupled. In 1935, the output reached 104,000 tons. But compared to Germany's oil consumption (3,322,000 tons in 1934), this output is very small.

Putting petroleum aside, let's look at the situation of lubricating oil (gasoline and petroleum spirits). In 1935, gasoline consumption reached 1,218,000 tons, and the output of gasoline refineries across the country was only 150,999 tons, a difference of more than one million tons. Fortunately, Germany is very rich in coal and lignite, and gasoline can be made from these two raw materials with the research of experts. The Leuna Works, which manufactures gasoline from coal slag, was established in 1929, and its annual output is expected to increase to 350,000 tons this year. In 1932, a certain factory in Nessebrug successfully tested the hydrogenation of lignite, and from then on, 300,000 tons of gasoline could be made from lignite every year. In October 1934, the Braunkohlen Cmpnyao, which is engaged in gasoline manufacturing, was established with a capital of 100 million marks.

From now on, Germany can manufacture 650,000 tons of synthetic gasoline, plus 150,000 tons of gasoline produced from oil wells, and the annual gasoline output can reach 800,000 tons. In a few more years, Germany's gasoline production can correspond to consumption. Unfortunately, synthetic gasoline is not suitable for aircraft engines; it is certainly impossible to supply all natural gasoline to aircraft engines.

Then, Germany's aviation problem has not yet been solved. But it will always be solved in the future. When this problem is solved, Germany's military power will at least double.

The production of another important fuel, petroleum spirits, is almost in line with needs: consumption is 320,000 tons, and production is 280,000 tons. As for alcohol, production is sufficient to supply consumption. In short, with the wisdom of chemists and the talent of technicians, Germany can soon make up for the lack of nature with synthetic products.

Industrial mobilization is one of the most complex problems in modern military affairs. The number of factories that manufacture military supplies in peacetime is insufficient during wartime. For example, at the end of 1914, the German artillery manufacturing industry produced 100 cannons per month. By June 1918, the German army needed 1,000 cannons per month, but there was still no shortage. To achieve this production standard, all factories in the country must be fully mobilized and participate in the manufacturing of an unlimited amount of military equipment.

Germany's industrial capabilities are unparalleled. The previous Great War has given us a lot of evidence: 3,000 white cannons, 11 million bombs, 14,000 machine guns, 250,000 rifles, and 12,000 tons of gunpowder. These quantities are not unusual because enemy countries can also equip them in the same amount. But the danger lies in the fact that Germany's entire industry is currently specializing in the manufacturing of military supplies, and its organization is the same as during wartime. Its mobilization period has ended, and the standstill period necessary for transforming factories when the war starts is almost non-existent, while in other countries, such a standstill period requires at least six months or more.

Strong industrial power, but insufficient raw materials—these are the two major characteristics of Germany. Germany can support itself. It can produce more and faster than any other European country. However, unless the goal of not relying on foreign imports of important raw materials is achieved, its huge efforts will always fail. When estimating Germany's combat power, the only shortcoming that can be considered is this. (Translated from Vu Weekly)

City News

Four Groups Elect National Assembly Representative Candidates Today; Agricultural and Commercial Members to Take Oath Tomorrow

The election of candidates for representatives to the National Assembly in this city will be held today by the labor union, lawyers, accountants, and medical professionals. Agricultural and fishing members will take the oath tomorrow. Members of trade associations will also take the oath tomorrow. Details are as follows:

Four Groups Elect: The time and location for the labor union, lawyers, accountants, and medical professionals to elect representative candidates today have been published in yesterday's newspaper and office notices. All executive personnel of the respective groups who have the right to attend the election must bring their own citizen certificate and group certificate in person and arrive at the venue on time to receive the election ticket. Use the signed, jointly signed method to fill in the appropriate personnel who meet Article 21 of the Election Law as candidates of this group. The quota is three for the labor union, ten for lawyers, five for accountants, and eight for medical professionals. After the election, personally cast the ballot into the ballot box that has been verified publicly. The polling officer and supervisor will affix a seal and wait for the legal period to open the ballot box and count the votes. As for the personnel supervising and managing the voting in each place today, the office has appointed Li Weixiong from the General Labor Union as the supervisor, and Wu Wenbang and Pan An as the managers. The three free professional groups of the Lawyers Association, etc., will be supervised by Cao Peizi and Chen Junyi, and managed by Hu Tianseng, Li Zhixiang, and Yuan Zengyu. (Reporter's note: The original text of Article 21 of the Election Law: The candidates for the professional groups in each province should have the following qualifications: (1) Have the qualifications of an elector; (2) Be at least twenty-five years old; (3) Have been engaged in the respective profession for more than three years; (4) Be a current member of the respective group. If the years of engaging in the profession in the previous item are intermittent, the combined periods shall be calculated.)

Agricultural and Fishing Members to Take Oath Tomorrow: The citizen oath registration of members of the agricultural association and fishing association was originally scheduled to be held today, but it has now been changed to be held tomorrow (30th) starting at 8:00 AM due to insufficient preparation. The location is still in the respective district agricultural association and the city fishing association. The office has already published a notice in the newspaper.

Oath Period for Chamber of Commerce: The office has also scheduled the citizen oath registration of members of more than 200 trade associations in the city to be held tomorrow (30th) starting at 9:00 AM and ending at 4:00 PM. The locations are divided into three places: (1) the City Chamber of Commerce at Tianhougong Bridge; (2) the Nanshi Branch Office of the City Chamber of Commerce on Zhonghua Road, Xiaonanmen; (3) the Renyi Shantang inside the Yanghuo Guild Hall at Dongxin Bridge. All members of the trade associations affiliated with the city's chamber of commerce must go to the above-mentioned locations nearby on time to complete the procedures so that they can participate in the voting in the future.

A Certain Standing Committee Member of the Municipal Party Headquarters Expresses Opinions on National Elections, Striving to Ensure Everyone Cherishes Their Civil Rights, Enhances Political Patriotism, and Participates in Elections

The Kuomintang News Agency reports that the national election procedures in this city have gradually entered the election stage. Social organizations have expressed very few opinions. Yesterday, a reporter from the Kuomintang News Agency visited a certain standing committee member of the municipal party headquarters to inquire about everything. The standing committee member expressed many opinions, which are recorded as follows. The standing committee member stated that the Central Government's convocation of the National Assembly to exercise the highest ruling power of the state is a clear indication that Chinese politics is gradually entering the constitutional stage from the period of political tutelage. Everyone knows the importance of its relation and the weight of its mission. Therefore, the successive plenary sessions of the Central Committee have repeatedly revised the draft constitution and precisely stipulated the principles of the election law, all with extensive consultation and careful consideration. Their painstaking efforts to attach importance to this national election and guide the people to exercise their political power are truly admirable. In terms of the electoral system, the regional system is adopted to seek its universality, and the professional system is adopted to seek its expertise. In terms of electoral methods, there are no restrictions on property, no discrimination based on gender, and no requirements for educational level. All adult citizens, regardless of gender, wealth, intelligence, or foolishness, have extensive rights to vote and be elected. Moreover, it reverses the previous step-by-step elections of primary and secondary elections, and instead uses universal and direct elections. Although it is in the period of political tutelage, circles must be added to indicate its scope, but the final decision still depends on the citizens of various places. It can be seen that the breadth and directness of this election right is opening the most glorious page in the history of Chinese elections. If the people of the whole country can enthusiastically participate, then the constitutional process will have a solid foundation. Otherwise, even if the country has a good system, it will often be counterproductive due to the improper use of personnel. There are many examples in the past. Although there are many enthusiastic and attentive people in promoting this national election, most of the general public is still indifferent. Some even refuse to register because they do not understand the content. The Municipal Party Headquarters has issued a letter to the people and scattered slogans and leaflets to call people's attention, but unfortunately, it has not been universal and in-depth. All groups have the responsibility of leading the people, and should widely advocate in this national election campaign, such as the instructions of election procedures, the identification of talent standards, and the discussion of national election issues. All efforts should be devoted to this. Schools should also compile national election issues into temporary teaching materials and teach them at any time, so that everyone can cherish their civil rights, enthusiastically participate in the grand event of national elections, enhance their political awareness, and develop their patriotic concepts. This is a rare opportunity to implement political education. As for the spirit of the election, it lies in electing the wise and capable. Therefore, the selection of talents is crucial. How to indicate standards for selection, how to establish a scope for selection, and how to publish political views for self-introduction are all things that professional groups from all walks of life can do at this time, so that talented people have the hope of being elected, and mediocre people have no way to advance by luck. People should use their talents, and the country can use them, so that the central government will not fail the original intention of protecting civil rights.

Revolutionary Elder You Lie Arrived in Shanghai from Hong Kong Yesterday Morning, Stating That He Came Here for Convalescence Due to Old Age and Illness, and Does Not Read Newspapers Often and Has No Opinions to Express on Current Affairs

The Xin Sheng News Agency reports that Mr. Yun Lie, a revolutionary elder, old friend of the late Premier, arrived in Shanghai from Hong Kong yesterday morning on the President Coolidge of the Dollar Steamship Lines. Representative Sun Ke and others went to the wharf to welcome him and made speeches. The details are recorded as follows:

Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday Morning Those who went to the wharf to welcome him yesterday were all friends. Therefore, few outsiders knew about this trip to Shanghai. They included a representative of Legislative Yuan President Sun Ke, as well as Zhou Binghua, Tan Haiqiu, Lu Jiale, Zhang Fan, Li Yiqin, Wang Haishan, Yun Wenwei, Wang Ziyang, and other people holding banners welcoming Mr. Yun Shaowen. The people who came with Yun included Secretary Ma Baimei, Doctor Chen Jing'an, Attaché Zhuo Wuchu, Li Zetang, Yin Yechun, and other five people. Yun was seasick on the ship and was very tired. When he got off the ship, he was helped onto a small boat and leaned on the sofa. At about 10 o'clock, he arrived at the New Customs Wharf and landed. He immediately took a car and returned to the Qiupu residence on Jessfield Road to rest.

You Lie's Demeanor Mr. Yun Lie is seventy-two years old this year. He is an old friend of the late Premier and made great contributions to the creation of the revolution. Mr. Yun participated in every righteous act. For example, when General Wu Luzhen launched an incident in Shijiazhuang and General Cai Songpo launched a revolt in Yunnan, both relied on Mr. Yun's persuasion and advocacy. After the Republic of China was established, he retired to practice medicine and help the world. He was indifferent to fame and wealth, honest and upright, fond of learning, and admired for his virtues. He is a rare person in the world. This time, he was fortunate to come to Shanghai for recuperation with the help of friends. Yesterday, Yun wore a white silk long gown, a black gauze mandarin jacket, cloth-soled shoes, and a long beard. He looked dignified, similar to the image of the most holy teacher Confucius. A reporter from the Xin Sheng News Agency insisted on an interview on the ship. Yun nodded frequently, indicating that the attendant should talk. According to him, Yun has been in Hong Kong for one or two decades and rarely goes out. This time, he plans to stay in Shanghai for a long time for recuperation and invites famous Chinese doctors for diagnosis and treatment. Because of his old age and physical discomfort, he usually only writes and plays chess in Hong Kong. The Shanghai residence is borrowed from Qiupu, No. 15 Jessfield Road, the residence of Tan Haiqiu.

Speeches A reporter from the Xin Sheng News Agency visited again in the afternoon yesterday and was received. He was told that because of his old age, he had no intention of traveling far. Recently, he often felt uncomfortable, and friends advised him to change places for recuperation. Therefore, he came here and did not assume other tasks. Before coming to Shanghai, many people in Hong Kong inquired about his views on the overall situation in the Southwest. However, the central government adhered to the principle of internal pacification and external resistance, and resolved the crisis in the Southwest without bloodshed, which is indeed a proposition to save the country and the people. He hopes very much to unify the national system, complete the national elections, and unify political views. We must use the power of the whole people to save the country in the shortest possible time. This is his greatest wish. He does not read newspapers often and is not clear about the current situation, so he has no opinions to express. He hopes for understanding. The reporter excused himself and left because the gentleman was mentally exhausted and it was not convenient to ask more questions.

Three Articles of the Trade Association Law, Requested for Interpretation, National Federation of Commerce Telegrams the Ministry of Industry

The National Federation of Commerce telegraphed the Ministry of Industry yesterday, "We have just received a letter from the Chongqing Mountain Goods Industry Trade Association stating that our association's business includes mountain goods such as cattle and sheep hides, pork floss, tung oil, and raw lacquer. Traditionally, the members of the trade association collect and transport them for export, which is a major part of Sichuan's foreign trade. The business rules for all items have been formulated and approved by the local government for implementation, and there have been no problems over the years. In addition to our association, there are no other organizations with the same nature. There are no business disputes among the various industry associations in the city. The prosperity of the market depends on its maintenance. Since recent years, a small number of our association's members have disobeyed the association's rules and seem to want to split the association, intending to separately form associations for tung oil, raw lacquer, and cattle hides, restricting our association's members from exporting and exclusively allowing them to purchase, transport, and export in order to manipulate market prices and monopolize business. They are now actively working to make this happen. The entire organization and the entire association's business will be torn apart. I and others are responsible and dare not remain silent. We hereby list the facts and request instructions: (1) After the establishment of a legally organized association, its business scope and rules have been submitted and approved by the local government. When other later associations have disputes over its business, according to the legal regulations, does the business belong to the first established association or the later established association? (2) After the establishment of a complete trade association of buyers, sellers, and brokers who are intermediaries in the same business, can they legally form separate trade associations for buyers, sellers, and brokers? If the law stipulates that separate associations cannot be formed, how should the already established association be requested to dissolve its organization? (3) In terms of both facts and law, the organization of its business cannot be allowed (such as when there is already an association with the same nature established earlier in the same area). However, due to temporary approval from the party headquarters and the local government, or the party headquarters and the local government are unaware of the actual situation, they issued organizational certificates and approved registration. How should the legally related trade associations request revocation and appeal to which level of party and government agencies, and what are the procedures? The above three items are all related to the interpretation of laws and regulations. We respectfully request clear instructions. If you would like to submit it to the Ministry of Industry for detailed explanation one by one so that we can follow, we would be grateful. Lin Kanghou, Chairman of the National Federation of Commerce of the Republic of China, respectfully."

Ministry of Communications Reduced Telegraph Rates, Effective September 1st

The Ministry of Communications instructed the Telegraph Bureau yesterday to investigate that our country's telegraph rates were previously divided into intra-provincial and inter-provincial. Since October 17, the current national uniform rates have been adopted, regardless of intra-provincial or inter-provincial, the same fees are charged. Although it is simple and convenient, since our country is vast, it is somewhat unfair to charge the same fees for telegrams sent to various places. Now, in order to facilitate people's communication and develop the telegraph bureau's business, the domestic telegraph rates have been revised as follows: (1) Domestic telegraph rates are divided into intra-provincial and inter-provincial. Ordinary telegrams in Chinese and vernacular language are 7 cents per word intra-provincial and 10 cents per word inter-provincial. (2) The regulations for reducing the fees for the name and address of the recipient of Chinese telegrams, which were implemented in January 23, stipulate that the name and address of the recipient, if not exceeding 15 words, will only be charged for 5 words, which is very convenient for people to send telegrams. However, this method, regardless of the number of words, charges for 5 words for those within 15 words, which is also not very fair. Now, the above method is revised and stipulated that the name and address of the recipient of all kinds of Chinese telegrams, except for those who use telegram registration numbers instead, will still be handled according to the telegram registration regulations. All will be charged as one word for every two words. If there is a remainder of less than two words, it will also be charged as one word. The revised rates and methods opened in the above two items have been approved by the Executive Yuan for record, and will be implemented from September 1, 25th year of the Republic. All relevant Articles 64, 82, and 84 of the domestic telegraph business regulations have also been revised and announced by the Ministry. In addition to the Ministry reprinting the domestic telegraph business regulations and the domestic telegraph rate list, which will be sent separately after printing, the revised articles of the domestic telegraph business regulations are attached for your compliance, and you are instructed to instruct all affiliated agencies and business offices to comply, prepare properly, and implement on schedule.

After receiving the order, the Telegraph Bureau heard that it has begun preparations and will implement it on schedule. From now on, the public will use telegrams and pay lower fees than the current rates. For example, sending to Zhonghua Bookstore in Hangzhou costs a total of 8 words. Zhonghua Bookstore in Hangzhou will be charged as 3 words, and "goods stop" will be charged as 2 words, costing a total of 35 cents. According to the current rates, Zhonghua Bookstore in Hangzhou must pay 5 words for 6 words, plus "goods stop" 2 words, totaling 7 words, which should cost 70 cents. Also, sending to Zhonghua Bookstore in Shanghai will also reduce the current rate by 20 cents.

Establishing a Grain Transportation and Sales Bureau: Soliciting Opinions from Rice Merchants

A report from the Da Gong News Agency states that the Ministry of Industry, with the intention of balancing domestic agricultural product transportation and sales, has been planning the establishment of a Grain Transportation and Sales Bureau for a long time. Due to various factors, implementation has been delayed. When Director Wu Dingchang of the Ministry of Industry was in Shanghai overseeing the affairs of the Agricultural Foundation Bureau, he took the opportunity to discuss the establishment of this bureau with Gu Xinyi, a leading figure among rice merchants. He also inquired about the reasons for the suspension of preparations for the government-supervised, merchant-operated Nine Provinces and Cities Grain Bureau from the previous year. Furthermore, he contacted key trade associations to establish the Grain Transportation and Sales Bureau, with the participation of merchant shares from the rice merchants' side, in order to prepare for the undertaking through joint cooperation between the government and merchants.

He therefore promised to convene a meeting of fellow traders to discuss it. The Bean and Rice Industry Association and the Miscellaneous Grain Industry Association recently held separate plenary sessions of their executive and supervisory committees. At the meetings, Gu gave a detailed report on the discussions with the Director, but did not put forward concrete proposals for discussion. Because this matter concerns the interests of all traders, a special representative conference will be convened soon to discuss concrete measures.

Grain Company Unlikely to Materialize: Regarding previous rumors that major rice merchants in this city were jointly investing in the organization of a large-scale grain company, the Da Gong News Agency reporter has been inquiring with reliable sources in recent days. The consensus is that the industry is currently relatively stable, and business operations are progressing smoothly. Setting up another grain company would be redundant and might lead to open and covert conflicts among traders. Moreover, in recent years, agricultural products have faced difficulties in finding outlets, prices have been low, and financial problems have made turnover difficult. It is anticipated that there is no good prospect for the future. Therefore, this organization is not likely to materialize in the short term.

Warehouses in Various Locations to Store Autumn Harvest: The National Economic Council and the Ministry of Finance are constructing agricultural product warehouses in Shanghai, Zhenjiang, Nanjing, Wuhu, Jiujiang, Changsha, Hankou, and other locations where agricultural products are concentrated. Construction is expected to be completed next month, with a decision to purchase and store grain during this year's autumn harvest. The equipment in these warehouses is part of a preliminary plan to control grain.

National Trade Deficit Exceeds Ten Million Yuan in July: Imports Total 74,915,086 Yuan, Exports Total 60,451,236 Yuan

According to yesterday's announcement by the Jianghai Customs, national foreign trade in July showed imports totaling 74,915,086 yuan in national currency, a decrease of 8,832,907 yuan compared to June, but an increase of 10,538,710 yuan compared to the same period last year. Exports in July totaled 60,451,236 yuan in national currency, an increase of 2,044,449 yuan compared to June and an increase of 14,492,309 yuan compared to the same period last year. The total import and export volume was 135,366,322 yuan, a decrease of 6,788,458 yuan compared to June and an increase of 25,031,019 yuan compared to the same period last year. The trade deficit was 14,463,850 yuan, a sharp decrease of 4 million yuan compared to the 18,417,449 yuan in the same period last year.

Country Statistics: According to customs statistics regarding major countries: (1) Imports: Imports from the United States totaled 16,551,000 yuan, a sharp increase of 2,361,000 yuan compared to June and a sharp increase of 4,583,000 yuan compared to the same period last year. Imports from Germany totaled 12,663,000 yuan, an increase of 1,393,000 yuan compared to June and an increase of 4,609,000 yuan compared to the same period last year. Imports from Japan totaled 9,369,000 yuan, a decrease of 1,520,000 yuan compared to June and an increase of 258,000 yuan compared to the same period last year. Imports from the United Kingdom totaled 8,632,000 yuan, a decrease of 2,866,000 yuan compared to June and an increase of 1,574,000 yuan compared to the same period last year. (2) Exports: Exports to the United States totaled 13,694,000 yuan, a decrease of 2,404,000 yuan compared to June and an increase of 3,095,000 yuan compared to the same period last year. Exports to Japan totaled 7,186,000 yuan, an increase of 538,000 yuan compared to June and an increase of 1,940,000 yuan compared to the same period last year. Exports to the United Kingdom totaled 6,178,000 yuan, a decrease of 751,000 yuan compared to June and an increase of 464,000 yuan compared to the same period last year. Exports to Germany totaled 4,459,000 yuan, an increase of 1,033,000 yuan compared to June and an increase of 1,817,000 yuan compared to the same period last year.

Trade Accumulation: Although both imports and exports of major commodities decreased in July compared to June, they increased compared to the same period last year. The total trade volume with Japan increased by 2,183,000 yuan, with the United Kingdom by 2,454,000 yuan, with the United States by 2,857,000 yuan, and with Germany by 8,304,000 yuan. From January to July of this year: (1) Imports: Imports from the United States totaled 98,628,000 yuan, a decrease of 20,690,000 yuan compared to the same period last year. Imports from Germany totaled 93,056,000 yuan, an increase of 30,118,000 yuan compared to the same period last year. Imports from Japan totaled 79,545,000 yuan, a decrease of 4,267,000 yuan compared to the same period last year. Imports from the United Kingdom totaled 63,469,000 yuan, an increase of 4,006,000 yuan compared to the same period last year. (2) Exports: Exports to the United States totaled 114,571,000 yuan, an increase of 39,004,000 yuan compared to the same period last year. Hong Kong ranked second, and Japan ranked third, with exports of 49,851,000 yuan, an increase of 14,650,000 yuan compared to the same period last year. Exports to the United Kingdom totaled 33,410,000 yuan, an increase of 8,036,000 yuan compared to the same period last year. Exports to Germany totaled 25,949,000 yuan, an increase of 8,414,000 yuan compared to last year.

Import and Export Goods: The value of imported goods in the first seven months of this year decreased by 76,000,000 yuan compared to the same period last year. Major imported goods that decreased included grains and flour, which decreased by approximately 78,000,000 yuan, and various cotton textiles, which decreased by 1 million yuan. Imported goods that increased included hemp, woolen textiles, hardware, vehicles, and sundries. On the export side, the value of exported goods in the first seven months of this year increased by 88,000,000 yuan compared to the same period last year. Major exported goods that increased included hides, furs, oils, silk, mineral ores, waxes, cotton yarn, hardware, and sundries.

Gold and Silver Imports and Exports: In the first seven months of this year, silver imports totaled 4,095,227 yuan, and gold imports totaled 927,000 gold units. Silver exports totaled 114,811,930 yuan, and gold exports totaled 5,182,438 gold units. The silver trade surplus for the seven months was 110,716,703 yuan (compared to 6,012,729 yuan in the same period last year), and the gold trade surplus was 4,255,438 gold units (compared to 13,856,933 gold units in the same period last year).

The New China Agricultural Society was organized by Tan Xihong, Director of the Forestry and Land Reclamation Department of the Ministry of Industry, and other national agricultural experts, with a total of over 500 members. It has made significant contributions to the reform of national agriculture. Resolution: Approved in principle, the scope of implementation to be determined by the next board of directors. Resolution: The society will recommend to the Ministry of Education that it make efforts to strengthen the equipment for higher agricultural education in the future and give full consideration to the establishment and cancellation of various departments. At about 4:00 PM, the discussion of society affairs ended. According to the meeting's agenda, the original schedule for the meeting was three days. However, attendees from various regions indicated that they had responsibilities to attend to, so the meeting schedule was changed with the approval of the general assembly, and the presentation of papers continued immediately to save time. The titles of the important papers and their authors are listed below: 1. Economic View of Monthly Rice Fertilizer Amount, Ma Shouzheng; 2. Correlation between Chemical Fertilizers and Agricultural Product Prices, Wu Xiangkui; 3. Correlation between Total Soil Phosphorus and Potassium and Their Available Amounts, Yu Hao; 4. The Effect of Phosphorus on the Growth of Black-Winged Aphids, Hu Shi; 5. Preliminary Report on the Comparative Study of Seedling Methods, Huang Xisu; 6. Cultivation Methods of Potatoes and Their Economic Value and Importance in National Defense, Luo Shiyi; 7. Research on Component Changes during Wheat Maturity, Mo Dingsen and Wu Yan; 8. Research on Wheat Grades in Jiangsu Province, Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau, Rice and Wheat Grading Office. After the papers were read, in accordance with the provisions of Article 5 of the Society's Constitution, Tan Xihong, Chang Zonghui, and Liu Hou were elected as election committee members. At about 6:00 PM, the chairman delivered the closing address and declared the meeting adjourned.

Shaanxi and Guizhou Included in Unified Tax Area: Effective from September 1st

The Ministry of Finance issued a circular stating: (1) Regarding merchants transporting and selling cigarettes in Shaanxi Province, the former Unified Tax Bureau issued an order in February of the 20th year of the Republic that all cigarettes must pay the unified tax and affix sufficient stamps before being allowed to be transported. The Ministry of Finance also consulted the Shaanxi Provincial Government on the matter of converting cigarette taxation and asked them to quickly prepare and negotiate the matter. The Ministry of Finance has now agreed with the Shaanxi Provincial Government to abolish all verification fees, surcharges, and transit donations for cigarettes. It has also been decided that from September 1st of this year, the province will be declared a unified tax area. The Ministry has telegraphed the provincial government to ensure that from that date, no further taxes or donations will be levied on cigarettes entering or passing through the province that have already paid the unified tax and affixed sufficient stamps. In addition to separate telegrams, the bureau is hereby ordered to inform its subordinates to comply accordingly. Tax Affairs Department of the Ministry of Finance. (2) Regarding cigarettes in Guizhou Province, the Ministry of Finance has ordered that the unified tax will be implemented from September 1st of this year. The province should be immediately included in the unified tax area. From September 1st, all cigarettes transported and sold from the unified tax area to Guizhou must pay the unified tax, affix sufficient stamps, and obtain a unified tax transportation permit before being allowed to be transported. No further taxes will be levied upon arrival in the province. Duty-free cigarettes transported to Guizhou before September 1st that arrive in the province after the implementation of the unified tax on September 1st should be subject to supplementary unified tax assessment by the Guizhou Provincial Finance Department in accordance with the unified tax rate, and stamps should be affixed before being allowed to be sold. In addition to separate telegrams, the bureau is hereby ordered to inform its subordinates to comply accordingly. Tax Affairs Department.

Ministry of Finance Approves Municipal Chamber of Commerce's Request for Stamp Tax on Temporary Silver and Cash Receipts

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce previously telegraphed the Ministry of Finance to inquire whether temporary silver and cash receipts should be subject to stamp tax. Yesterday, the Ministry of Finance issued approval No. 10515 of the Tax Affairs Department, stating: "The Geng Dai telegram has been noted. It is an established principle of stamp tax that a certificate should not be taxed twice. However, many stores issue a so-called 'temporary receipt' after receiving silver and cash, without affixing a stamp. Over the years, these receipts are not collected and exchanged for formal receipts. When they are detected and subject to a fine, they claim to be temporary receipts in an attempt to be clever. The tax exemption column in item 2 of the stamp tax rate table does not stipulate that temporary receipts are exempt from stamping. This is the reason. As for the permit for commercial registration issued by the government, a formal permit must be exchanged after a considerable period of time, which is different from the above situation. The request to be exempt from stamping should not be considered." This approval.

Please Use Domestically Produced Mao Bian Paper for National Election Ballots: Request from Shanghai Citizens Chen Xing-sun and Others: To Set an Example, Promote Domestic Products, and Cultivate the National Foundation

Shanghai citizens Chen Xing-sun, Feng Yangqing, and others, in view of the upcoming election of representatives to the National Assembly and the vast amount of paper needed for ballots, telegraphed the Nanjing National Election Headquarters requesting the use of domestically produced Mao Bian paper to save resources and support domestic products. The original text is as follows: (Omitted honorifics) With the election of representatives to the National Assembly imminent, a vast amount of paper is needed for the ballots. We have heard that foreign newsprint may be used for printing. Upon hearing this, we felt it was absolutely unacceptable. The government has repeatedly emphasized the promotion of domestic products, and the election of National Assembly representatives is a major national event. Using foreign newsprint for the ballots is not only contrary to the government's policy of promoting domestic products, but also encourages the people to become accustomed to using foreign products. Moreover, since the ballots are written on one side, it is easier to dry when writing on domestically produced Mao Bian paper. Even considering the price of newsprint, which costs 3.30 yuan per ream, domestically produced Mao Bian paper is only 3.10 yuan per ream, which is more economical. To abandon this economical and suitable domestically produced Mao Bian paper and use foreign newsprint would only cause huge amounts of money to flow to foreign lands, which is contrary to the government's long-standing policy of promoting domestic products and cultivating the national foundation. We dare not remain silent on this humble opinion. Therefore, we appeal to your office to order your subordinates and instruct the organizers to use domestically produced Mao Bian paper for printing the ballots for the National Assembly representatives, in order to maintain domestic products and set an example. We express our urgent request and hope for your kind consideration.

All Silk Factories in the City Open Full-Day Shifts: White Filature Prices Slightly Higher: Autumn Silk Affected

Silk reeling factories in various districts of the city previously switched to half-day shifts from July 1st due to the intense heat and inability to work full days. Now that it is autumn and the weather is cooler, they have all resumed full-day shifts from the 25th of this month. The daily working hours are from 5:00 AM to 11:30 AM and from 12:30 PM to 5:30 PM. Currently, there are silk factories operating in the city, including: (Xinzha District) Dafeng, Chengfeng, Hongtai, Xieyu, Yichang, Fuchang, Dacheng, Meifeng, Dongxiang, and 17 others; (Zhabei District) Yutai, Hongchang, Huashun, Shaoxing, Xinglun, Hengtai, Yufeng, Jiufeng, Qiaoyuan, and 15 others; (Hongkou District) Yiji, Zhongguo, Tianmai, Yuchang, Baoyu, Liyuan, Xiangcheng, Changji, Zhongyu, and 9 others; (Concession District) Xinchang, Yihe, and 2 others; (Hunan District) Guangyuan, Baotai, and 2 others, for a total of 45. In the overseas silk market, the highest quality white filature from Shanghai is selling for around 660 yuan per dan, a slight increase from before. Autumn silk is affected by the unfavorable weather, but since the spring silk harvest was abundant and the number of silkworm breeders this year has increased by more than half compared to before, a shortage is not likely to be felt again.

Oath administrator Sun Honglin delivered a speech, stating that the appointments of President Lu and Chief Prosecutor Zhu were announced one month apart. The prosecutorial powers are independent of the court. The court and the prosecution should advance simultaneously and work together. Both gentlemen have rich knowledge and experience, and with their joint efforts, they will surely live up to expectations. President Lu has been in office for two months, reorganizing court affairs. Today, as a result of my and President Zhu's visit, there has been much progress. Chief Prosecutor Zhu has not been in office for long, but in the future, he will surely achieve excellence and greatness. Oath administrator Lin Meiyan of the City Party Department delivered a speech, hoping to improve the spirit of justice and create a Party-oriented judiciary for the benefit of all citizens. Finally, a group photo was taken, and the event concluded.

The Unidentified Male Corpse in Wuxi Almost Resulted in a Wrongful Conviction: Yu Lili Was Wrongfully Imprisoned, Wu Piaoping Stepped Forward to Reveal the Truth

Wu Piaoping, secretary of the Shanghai Sutain Opera Research Association (originally named Zhang Zishi, from Dachang Township in northern Shanghai, 40 years old), is usually involved in Sutain Opera performances, so he is very familiar with the leading actors. When Wuxi Great World opened, Wu was invited by Yang Liansheng to Wuxi to perform Sutain Opera. Wu introduced Shi Xiangyun and Yu Lili (also known as Xiao Wawa, wife of Yu Ruixiang) to join and perform together. Later, because Shi and Yu competed for the top billing, disputes arose, and Wu was severely criticized. On the 8th of this month, wearing a vest, he left without saying goodbye, traveled from Wuxi to Suzhou, borrowed travel expenses from a friend, took a car to Shanghai, and returned to his home in Dachang Township. Unexpectedly, on the 13th, an unidentified male corpse with knife wounds was discovered in Xiadian Township, Wuxi. People suspected that the corpse was the missing Wu Piaoping, leading to Yu Lili being suspected of murder. She was arrested by the Wuxi Court, causing a stir in the city. Wu, residing in the countryside, eventually found it unsustainable and took a car to Shanghai to borrow travel expenses from Zhu Guoliang, a famous Sutain Opera performer living in Baokang Lane, Beijing Road, intending to seek work elsewhere. At that time, Yu's mother, Xu, entrusted a friend, Wu Shutang, to come to Shanghai to inquire about Wu's whereabouts from Zhu (because Zhu was a friend of Wu). Thus, Wu and Wu met. Wu Shutang told him about the suspected murder case in Wuxi. Wu Piaoping then traveled with Wu Shutang by car to Wuxi overnight to explain the facts to the court. After questioning by the prosecutor, Yu was released on bail.

Slum Dwellers Association Asks the Municipal Council to Build Public Housing Quickly, Expressing Improved Living Conditions, Five Resolutions Were Agreed Upon

The Shanghai Slum Dwellers Association sent a letter to the Municipal Council yesterday, stating that slum dwellers are a special group of impoverished people who cannot afford to rent houses and can only build simple shacks to temporarily shelter from the wind and rain. They go out to work hard during the day and stay in the shacks at night to barely survive their poverty-stricken lives. Since your esteemed council has proposed the limited demolition of slums, we have been greatly shocked. As far as the daily life of our slum dwellers is concerned, it is already difficult and precarious. If we are forced to relocate again, we will be displaced, and the misery will be unbearable to witness. We believe that the council's desire to demolish slums is based on concerns about urban appearance and hygiene. However, in today's situation, the economic downturn is shaking the entire city. Even prosperous areas such as Nanjing Road and Avenue Edward VII are seeing an increasing number of vacant houses. Notices of clearance and court seals are visible everywhere. This is actually the biggest damage to the city's appearance, which your council has not yet taken into account. Furthermore, after the demolition of our slums, we will not be able to afford to rent houses and will inevitably wander the streets, sleeping anywhere. This is the opposite of your council's desire to improve the city's appearance. In terms of hygiene, our slum dwellers are also aware and will automatically carry out tasks such as cleaning dirt and dredging ditches, in order to gradually improve hygiene matters. We believe that the municipal authorities should take into account the needs of all citizens in the area and provide universal protection. Our slum dwellers are ignorant and foolish, but they work hard and serve in urban construction. Even if we dare not claim credit, we have done no wrong. At this time of economic depression and increasing hardship, we are terrified to hear of the demolition order. Our association is entrusted by slum dwellers in various districts to improve the lives of slum dwellers. For the sake of the livelihoods of the poor and the appearance and hygiene of the city, we have made the following resolutions: (1) In the future, our slum dwellers will automatically limit and not increase the number of slums. (2) If the landlord builds houses or the Municipal Council needs to open roads, the slum dwellers will immediately relocate. (3) Comply with the guidance of the municipal authorities to improve sanitation facilities. (4) Request the Municipal Council to revoke the demolition order to ensure a livelihood. (5) Request the Municipal Council to allocate funds as soon as possible to build public housing to accommodate the poor, in order to eliminate slums in phases. All cases have been recorded. This matter concerns the life and death of our slum dwellers and we cannot remain silent. We specially send this letter to you, respectfully requesting that you consider the economic depression and the suffering of the poor, and approve the adoption of our foolish suggestions and implement them separately. We will be deeply grateful. Addressed to the Public Concession Municipal Council.

Shen Weizhi Discovered Stone Tools in Huzhou, Lent Them to the Wuyue History and Geography Society for Exhibition, Counting Dozens of Items

The Wuyue History and Geography Society, presided over by Wei Juxian, will hold an exhibition soon. It is said that dozens of stone tools will be among them, which were collected by Shen Weizhi, secretary-general of the business school in the downtown area of ​​Shanghai University, and temporarily co-exhibited. According to Shen Weizhi, a total of forty-eight items were lent to the Wuyue History and Geography Society, including a complete stone awl, seven complete stone arrowheads, eleven incomplete ones, seven complete stone coins, one stone axe, one stone yue, fourteen broken stone tools, and four broken copper pieces. These stone tools were all collected by Shen in his hometown of Huzhou, near the Qianshanyang Lake Beach. Shen has been very interested in these antiquities since he was a child, so he has repeatedly collected and researched them, with unique insights. The above-mentioned dozens of newly acquired items were all collected from 1934 to the present. It is said that the collected objects are all newly unearthed. According to research, the oldest ones are from the late Shang and early Zhou dynasties. This type of discovery is of great significance to Chinese culture. Whether the source of Chinese culture is from south to north or from north to south has become a topic of discussion for those who pay attention to this issue. However, the discovery of these historical antiquities in Huzhou will help provide new materials for research. This discovery also shows that there have been major changes in the geographical situation of China over the past 5,000 years. Therefore, although not many items have been collected, their value is very high. Shen still has many scattered unearthed ancient stone tools and other collections, but their historical value is shallow, so they are not mentioned. It is said that Shen is still working hard to collect them, and it is expected that there will be new discoveries in the future, which will make a significant contribution to academics.

Lu Jingshi Mediates: Rent Reduction in Nine Mu Area

More than 300 new residential buildings in various lanes of the nine mu area on Minquan Road and Renyi Jizhiren Road in Lushang Garden of Shanghai belong to the property of Anhe Company. Since the entry of special business owners into the area, the market has become prosperous. However, merchants who rent there often bear high rents, and are extorted for tips and bad rules by the rental agency office when they move in, ranging from thousands of yuan to at least several hundred yuan. Therefore, the public was indignant and jointly presented a petition to the South District Rent Reduction Association for justified negotiation. Now, Mr. Lu Jingshi has been appointed as mediator. After Anhe Company suspended the rental agency office that collected tips for thorough investigation, it also reduced the original rent of 1100 yuan per double building to 77.5 yuan to accommodate the difficulties of the merchants. The general merchants heard that the house prices there are cheaper than in remote areas, and it is also suitable for opening shops and living at home. Therefore, only a few houses are left in the more than 300 residential buildings. It is also learned that Anhe Company has issued a notice that merchants who want to rent there must not pay tips again. If the rental agency office deliberately makes things difficult, they can directly report to the company for strict punishment, to eliminate bad rules and create a new example for renting houses in Shanghai.

Guan Mingyuan, who lives at No. 48 Dashiqiao, Beiping, cohabited with his wife, Ms. Liu (32 years old, from Beiping). In the beginning, their relationship was fairly harmonious. They had a daughter, aged 13, named Yanqin. In the first month of this year, Tian Yu, a Beiping native who worked as a boxing master, had stayed at Guan's home because he and Guan were from the same hometown and were friends. He reported it to the Beiping Public Security Bureau, which sent a letter to the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau. At 9:50 PM the night before, two detectives, No. 107 and No. 113, reported to the Chengdu Road Police Station and assisted Chinese and foreign detectives in arresting Tian Yu, Guan Ms. Liu, and Guan Yanqin together at No. 167 Dagu Road and detaining them in the police station for separate detention. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the 8th Criminal Court of the First Special Court. Police Station lawyer Zhang Tianyin stated the previous situation. Then, a detective from the Municipal Public Security Bureau filed a case and requested transfer, claiming that he had not prepared official documents due to the short time. Tian Yu only admitted to staying temporarily at Guan Mingyuan's house in Beiping and denied instigating Ms. Liu to abscond. Guan Ms. Liu confessed that she could not bear to live with her husband because of his abuse, so she had no choice but to take her daughter to Shanghai in early February, seek refuge with Tian Yu's family for temporary residence, and seek Tian's help to find ways to maintain a living, and there was no improper behavior. Judge Huang Risheng checked the confession and instructed that Tian Yu and others should still be detained separately until the official documents from the Municipal Public Security Bureau arrive next Monday for further verification.
